### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-lewicasd.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Lewica (S&D).

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 0 | 4% | 100% | Last Result |
| 1 | 0% | 96% |  |
| 2 | 2% | 96% |  |
| 3 | 14% | 94% |  |
| 4 | 25% | 80% |  |
| 5 | 37% | 55% | Median |
| 6 | 15% | 18% |  |
| 7 | 3% | 3% |  |
| 8 | 0.2% | 0.2% |  |
| 9 | 0% | 0% |  |
